		every_state = { # if full decentralization happened
					limit = {
						OR = {
							is_core_of = SLV
							is_core_of = CRO
							is_core_of = BOS
							is_core_of = MNT
							is_core_of = KOS
							is_core_of = MAC
							is_core_of = VOJ
						}
						NOT = { is_core_of = ROOT }
					}
					add_core_of = ROOT
				}
			YUG_remove_croatian_opposition_effect = yes
			set_global_flag = no_croat_opposition
			every_other_country = { # as to not make a mess
				limit = {
					has_event_target = released_nation_target
					is_subject_of = ROOT
				}
				ROOT = { 
					annex_country = {
						target = PREV
						transfer_troops = yes
					}
				}
			}
			add_offsite_building = { type = industrial_complex level = 1 }
			add_offsite_building = { type = arms_factory level = 4 }
			add_equipment_to_stockpile = {
				type = convoy
				amount = 100
				producer = YUG
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					has_power_balance = {
						id = YUG_power_balance_centralization
					}
				}
				remove_power_balance = {
					id = YUG_power_balance_centralization
				}
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					has_power_balance = {
						id = YUG_power_balance_neutrality
					}
				}
				remove_power_balance = {
					id = YUG_power_balance_neutrality
				}
			}
			set_power_balance = {
				id = YUG_chetnik_partisan_conflict
				left_side = YUG_chetnik_side
				right_side = YUG_partisan_side
				set_value = 0
			}
			country_event = better_yugo_resistance.1
			hidden_effect = {
				
				every_state = { # if full decentralization happened
					limit = {
						OR = {
							is_core_of = SLV
							is_core_of = CRO
							is_core_of = BOS
							is_core_of = MNT
							is_core_of = KOS
							is_core_of = MAC
							is_core_of = VOJ
						}
						NOT = { is_core_of = ROOT }
					}
					add_core_of = ROOT
				}
				### THE FOLLOWING CODE TRIES TO MAKE A REALISTIC SPLIT OF YUGOSLAVIA THAT MIMICS WHAT HAPPENED IRL
				if = {
					limit = {
						owns_state = 102
					}
					if = {
						limit = {
							has_war_with = GER
						}
						GER = { set_state_controller = 102 }
					}
					else_if = {
						limit = {
							has_war_with = AUS
						}
						AUS = { set_state_controller = 102 }
					}
					else_if = {
						limit = {
